The surprise is the bed in the hotel, which seems to have a kind of magic that allows people to fall asleep quickly and peacefully. The most noteworthy thing is, of course, the service. During my stay, the person who impressed me the most was the male manager who was always busy and a little older (I don't know if this name is accurate). He really served the guests attentively. name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Cozy Standard Room
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:2.2
posted:Posted February 12, 2024
msg:During the Spring Festival, there were many people in Taierzhuang Ancient City. We came on the first day of the ***** New Year. There were enough people. On the second day of the ***** New Year, there were more people and the performance was good.

Facilities: We were in Building B, which is relatively old. The towels were of the rigid series, not white and not soft, and the sink was old and yellow.

Hygiene: It's okay. My daughter said it was smelly when she just entered the lobby. It was indeed a bit old. The carpet in the room felt dusty when you stepped on it, and there was dust. It needs to be cleaned. My cough has worsened again in the past two days.

Environment: The environment is average. The room has no heating and relies on air conditioning for heating. It must be cold in winter. It is very dry when the air conditioner is turned on.

Service: The ancient city is full of slabs of stone, the kind of slabs dug in pits. Boxes and strollers cannot be pushed. They are bumpy. Let us go from Xiaonanmen. It says that there is a car to pick us up, but there is no car. I carried the box, which was very heavy. Someone said that someone would pick me up, but I didn't. I was encouraged by saying that it was not far, just 10 minutes. I believed it. When I arrived at the hotel, I was almost exhausted. We finally arrived, and thought we could push our suitcases on the flat floor, but they arranged us in Building B. A waiter led us and smiled at me, saying "go this way", but he didn't help me carry the suitcase. I just watched, and climbed over a stone bridge to the second floor (there was no elevator). I had to carry the suitcases myself. So do you think they have a sense of service? The answer is not at all.
